## Re: Geodis: Rate Asia / Callao \- Project Cago

Dear Masuda san,

Thks for your message. Pls let me comment:

Is this a bid (with multiple rounds), or a direct negotiation?

SR: It is a direct negotiation with Geodis \- Projects

Pls kindly note cargo handled by Projects is different. Even though this

cargo is in dry cntrs. the way of negotiation is the projects way, very

quick.

Note: Regarding Geodis, which is a GKA, it has been internally agreed in

this period's game plan that 50% will go to NAC and the remaining 50% to

FAK. If this is a bid and NAC, then we would need the same volume of FAK

business to match.

SR: Pls this cargo should note be considered under the forwarding

agreement. Even Though this cargo is dry cntrs.  it is a project cargo

handled by the project division of Geodis. They work in a different way.

Geodis acting as the BCO, or on behalf of the shipper (Calpataru / ISA REP)?

SR: Geodis is acting as owner of the project at Peru they handle the

shipping, local warehousing, local transport, etc. It is  a complex project

at Peru. They were awarded by ISA.

For us the most important points are that Geodis Peru has full authority to

decide their suppliers (including shipping lines) and will issue HB/L.

Is the customer expecting a long-term contract for 2 years, as mentioned in

your email?

SR: Geods already has an agreement with CMA for 2 years validity with

floating BAF. Their target is to get the same with a second carrier. But if

you consider it tis oo long, I can try with 1 year validity and see if they

can  accept it.

What is the target rate level that the customer expects us to match? (

CMA’s offer  USD 1,500/20’ and USD 1,600/40’ ?) Please note that this level

is low compared to the current our rate level for tender.

SR: USD 1,500/20’ and USD 1,600/40 but subject to BAF changes.is their

target. My suggestion is to get as closer as possible.

Pls kindly note the validity requested is from Oct 2025 till Oct 2027,

cargo?

Dear CLAUDIA,

Thanks for your message.

Please note that although Lumicenter is included in the AP, we have

temporarily capped the NOR volume at 50 units per week. Due to the heavy

overloading during the Golden Week holidays, there is now a heavy surplus

of NOR equipment in Callao, and we need to control the flow from Asia to

avoid further imbalance.

This measure is not related to the AP itself, but purely an operational

control to stabilize the equipment situation at destination.

Therefore, we regret to inform that we will decline this request for now,

but we will revisit the acceptance again in November once the situation

normalizes.

MAKASSAR \-KAMT2509N ETD THLCH 2 SEP, so its route only has 1 transhipment

momentum.
